  168. # [01:34] <billm> cpearce: hey. I just have a basic GMP question. what are node IDs and tags?
  169. # [01:35] <cpearce> a node Id is a value that corresponds to the origin of the document in which the GMP is running, and the "top level", or "URL bar" origin. it's randomly generated the first time that origin pair accesses EME, and it's cleared when storage is cleared.
  170. # [01:36] <cpearce> billm: "tags" are the APIs or properties of APIs that GMPs say thsy support
  171. # [01:36] <cpearce> billm: like "I support video decoding for h264" etc
  172. # [01:36] <billm> cpearce: where does the node ID get generated?
